[2;36m                    [0m         during PDF-to-text OCR processing. Untrusted input flowing into                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` in Apache PDFBox’s `OCRStreamEngine` allows                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue type: OS Command Injection [1m([0mflagged as `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` by     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Jazzer[1m)[0m.                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - What happened: The fuzzer supplied crafted PDF content to the OCR harness         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`PDFOCRFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m, which ultimately invoked                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `OCRStreamEngine.doOCR`. During this method’s execution, a `ProcessBuilder` was     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         started with arguments that include attacker‐controlled data. Jazzer’s              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `OsCommandInjection` sanitizer caught the unsafe `[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` call.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Key observations:                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The exception originates in                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.OsCommandInjection.processImplStartHook`   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mOsCommandInjection.kt:[1;36m60[0m[1m)[0m, indicating detection of untrusted data passed to an     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         external process.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The vulnerable call chain:                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             – `PDFOCRFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` [1m([0mPDFOCRFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:75[0m[1m)[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         `runTesseract` [1m([0mOCRStreamEngine.jav[1;92ma:165[0m[1m)[0m → `doOCR` [1m([0mOCRStreamEngine.jav[1;92ma:190[0m[1m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             – Inside `doOCR`, a `ProcessBuilder` is constructed and started.                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The harness merely drives the code under test; the vulnerability resides in how [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `OCRStreamEngine` builds and runs OS commands.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code areas for investigation:                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • `org.apache.pdfbox.ocr.OCRStreamEngine.doOCR` [1m([0maround line [1;36m190[0m[1m)[0m – inspect       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ProcessBuilder invocation and argument construction.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • `runTesseract` [1m([0mline [1;36m165[0m[1m)[0m and upstream methods [1m([0m`processPage`, `processPages`,  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The initial issue is a Jazzer-detected security finding: an OS command injection    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[1m)[0m triggered when `OCRStreamEngine.runTesseract`       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         invokes an external Tesseract executable using attacker-controlled data. A patch    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         was attempted to validate and constrain the executable path by converting it to a   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Path`, checking existence, file type, and executable permissions, and throwing an  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exception if validation failed. After applying the patch, Maven Checkstyle failed   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         with a parse error in `OCRStreamEngine.java` [1m([0m“mismatched input [32m'String'[0m expecting  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m';'[0m”[1m)[0m, indicating a syntax or formatting issue in the modified code.                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - A Jazzer fuzzing run crashed with                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: OS Command           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Injection`.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Stack trace shows the vulnerability arises in `OCRStreamEngine.runTesseract`,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         which builds and starts a `ProcessBuilder` with a path derived from PDF document    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         metadata [1m([0m`TESSERACT_PATH_KEY`[1m)[0m or a default.                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Because the executable path originates from untrusted input, an attacker could    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         inject arbitrary OS commands.                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Important Observations                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The vulnerable code is in `org.apache.pdfbox.ocr.OCRStreamEngine.doOCR` →         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `runTesseract` → `doOCR`, leading to `[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The fuzzer input explores metadata values and triggers the injection.             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The code uses a raw string path for the executable without validating content or  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         filesystem properties.                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The patch replaces the two-line retrieval of `actualTessPath` with logic that:    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. Reads `candidateTessPath` from document metadata.                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. If non-null and non-empty, converts it to a `Path` [1m([0m`tessExecutablePath`[1m)[0m.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Checks `Files.exists`, `Files.isRegularFile`, and `Files.isExecutable` on      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `tessExecutablePath`.                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. Throws `IOException` on failure.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. Otherwise, falls back to the original `tesseractPath`.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m6[0m. Converts `tessExecutablePath` back to an absolute-string `actualTessPath`.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The contextual diff around line [1;36m156[0m of `OCRStreamEngine.java` was:                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```diff                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - String actualTessPath = [1;35mpdDocument.getDocumentInformation[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            -        [1;35m.getCustomMetadataValue[0m[1m([0mTESSERACT_PATH_KEY[1m)[0m;                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - if [1m([0mactualTessPath == null || [1;35mactualTessPath.isEmpty[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            -     actualTessPath = tesseractPath;                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - [1m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            + String candidateTessPath = pdDocument                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +     [1;35m.getDocumentInformation[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +     [1;35m.getCustomMetadataValue[0m[1m([0mTESSERACT_PATH_KEY[1m)[0m;                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            + Path tessExecutablePath;                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            + if [1m([0mcandidateTessPath != null && ![1;35mcandidateTessPath.isEmpty[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +     tessExecutablePath = [1;35mPaths.get[0m[1m([0mcandidateTessPath[1m)[0m;                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +     if [1m([0m![1;35mFiles.exists[0m[1m([0mtessExecutablePath[1m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +         || ![1;35mFiles.isRegularFile[0m[1m([0mtessExecutablePath[1m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +         || ![1;35mFiles.isExecutable[0m[1m([0mtessExecutablePath[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +         throw new [1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0m[32m"Invalid tesseract executable path: "[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +             + candidateTessPath[1m)[0m;                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +     [1m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            + [1m}[0m else [1m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            +     tessExecutablePath = [1;35mPaths.get[0m[1m([0mtesseractPath[1m)[0m;                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            + [1m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            + String actualTessPath = [1;35mtessExecutablePath.toAbsolutePath[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - After this change, invoking Maven with `mvn checkstyl[1;92me:c[0mheck` produced:           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           IllegalStateException occurred while parsing file                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [33m...[0m[35m/[0m[95mOCRStreamEngine.java[0m:[1;92m159:8[0m: mismatched input [32m'String'[0m expecting [32m';'[0m:          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         - The error pinpoints a syntax/formatting error at line [1;36m159[0m, column [1;36m8[0m, preventing   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         successful build.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The codebase was flagged by Jazzer for an OS command injection vulnerability:       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attacker-controlled data could reach a `[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` call in             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mOCRStreamEngine.runTesseract[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`. A patch was attempted to validate the          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Tesseract executable path using `java.nio.file` APIs [1m([0me.g., `[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`,          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mFiles.exists[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`, catching `InvalidPathException`[1m)[0m before invoking                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ProcessBuilder`. When applying this patch, the build failed under the Maven        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Checkstyle plugin with an `InputMismatchException`: an `import` statement appeared  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         mid‐class [1m([0mline [1;36m43[0m[1m)[0m, causing a “mismatched input [32m'import'[0m expecting [32m'[0m[32m}[0m[32m'[0m” error and  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         blocking compilation.                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer fuzzer detected an OS command injection                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[1m)[0m in `[1;35mOCRStreamEngine.runTesseract[0m[1m([0mPath image[1m)[0m`.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The code builds a command line: it takes `actualTessPath` [1m([0mfrom PDF metadata   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         or default[1m)[0m, then calls `[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - No validation or sanitization of the path string allows an attacker to supply  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         malicious input, leading to remote code execution.                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Key Observations in the Stack Trace                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The crash originates in                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.OsCommandInjection.processImplStartHook`,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         triggered by `[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The call hierarchy leads from `[1;35mOCRStreamEngine.doOCR[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` →                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mrunTesseract[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` → `[1;35mdoOCR[0m[1m([0mactualTessPath, [33m...[0m[1m)[0m`.                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The fuzzer harness [1m([0m`PDFOCRFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m supplies PDF input,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         which may carry a crafted metadata value for `TESSERACT_PATH_KEY`.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The patch introduces validation logic in `[1;35mOCRStreamEngine.runTesseract[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`:  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Retrieve `candidateTessPath` from metadata.                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • If non‐empty, convert to `Path tessExecutablePath =                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mPaths.get[0m[1m([0mcandidateTessPath[1m)[0m`.                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Check `[1;35mFiles.exists[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`, `[1;35mFiles.isRegularFile[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`,                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mFiles.isExecutable[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`.                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Catch `InvalidPathException`, wrap into `IOException`.                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Otherwise, fallback to the preconfigured `tesseractPath`.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Finally, derive `actualTessPath =                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtessExecutablePath.toRealPath[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - New imports added:                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              import java.nio.file.Files;                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              import java.nio.file.InvalidPathException;                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              import java.nio.file.Paths;                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Original simple assignment of `actualTessPath` was removed.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Result                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Applying the patch triggered a Checkstyle/Java‐parsing error:                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              IllegalStateException occurred while parsing file [33m...[0m[35m/[0m[95mOCRStreamEngine.java[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [1;92m43:0[0m: mismatched input [32m'import'[0m expecting [32m'[0m[32m}[0m[32m'[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This indicates the `import` statements were placed inside the class body [1m([0mat   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         line [1;36m43[0m[1m)[0m, not at the top of the file, violating Java syntax rules and Checkstyle    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         configuration.                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - As a result, the Maven build stops, and the patch cannot be validated or       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         tested further.                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Areas for Further Investigation                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The structure of `OCRStreamEngine.java`: confirm where imports should be       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         declared [1m([0mfile head vs. inside class[1m)[0m.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The `[1;35mrunTesseract[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` and `[1;35mdoOCR[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` implementations to understand all     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         code paths invoking `ProcessBuilder`.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The definition and usage of `tesseractPath` and related configuration in the   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         codebase.                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Any other places in the code where external commands are executed with         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         user‐controllable data.                                                             [2m                [0m
